MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

S. Ramamoorthy, A male child born to Thiru S. Shanmugavel, on 29th May 1983 residing at No. 156, Vellai Gate
near Pallava Engineering College, Thimmasamudram, Kancheepuram-631 502, has been living as a female after an
elaborate sexual reassignment surgery By Dr. V. Jayaraman by this, I may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be
known as S. AMIRTHA.
Kancheepuram,
8th June 2017.

S. RAMAMOORTHY

T. Suresh a male child born to Thangaraj, Hindu and born on 11th February 1991 residing at No. 25, Porchelizien
Street, Ullagaram, Chennai-600 061, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery
on 3rd December 2016, Chennai Ortho Centre, 12, Ramakrishna Nagar Extension, Radakrishnan Salai, Valasaravakkam,
Chennai, Tamil Nadu 600 095, Surgery by Dr. V. Jayaraman, (Regn: 32070) Former Professor of Plastic Surgery, Kilpauk,
Medical College of Head of upgraded Burns Unit, Kilpauk, Medical College, Hospital, Chennai-600 010. By this I may be
treated as a Female and henceforth be known as T. THANISHKA.

Chennai,
8th June 2017.

T. SURESH.
